\n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div><div class=\"wpb_row row green home-header vc_custom_1403279027389\" style=\"color:#ffffff;\">\n\t<div class=\"columns twelve wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"wpb_row row section-header\">\n\t<div class=\"columns three wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"nv-skin mediawrap    \"><div class=\"container \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><a href=\"/hydroponic-growing-systems/\" title=\"\" target=\"_self\" class=\"\"><img src=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wp-content/uploads/hydro_rev-2xvorf4cpy50f2wih23ax6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"\" height=\"\" style=\"visibility: visible; opacity: 1;\"></a></div></div></div></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\n\t<div class=\"columns nine wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h1><a name=\"hydro\"></a><br>\n<a title=\"Hydroponic Growing Systems\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-growing-systems/\">Hydroponic Systems</a></h1>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div><div class=\"wpb_row row\">\n\t<div class=\"columns eight wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\">Hydroponic Systems</h2>\n<h2><strong>First visit our <a title=\"Hydroponic systems reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-growing-systems\">Hydroponics Systems</a>&nbsp;Master Page</strong>&nbsp;to get a run down on all the different hydro systems available to you.</h2>\n<p>Hydroponics simply&nbsp;means that the plants can grow without soil. They will usually grow in an inert medium and all of their nutrient requirements will come straight from the water they are added to. After choosing your <a title=\"Hydro set-up\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-growing-systems/\">hydro setup</a> you will need to pick what&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/growing-medium\">growing medium</a>&nbsp;to grow your marijuana in; some prefer the organic nature of good soil and others like the more synthetic such as rock wool and perlite. Apart from this difference the way you set up your <a title=\"Grow room planning\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/grow-room/\">grow room</a> will be the same.</p>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>We always suggest buying a <a title=\"Grow box reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/grow-box\">Grow Box</a>, <a title=\"Grow tent reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/grow-tent\">Grow Tent</a> or <a title=\"Stealth hydroponic kits\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/stealth-grow-box\">Stealth hydroponic kit</a>&nbsp;from experts.</strong></h2>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>The advice from companies like&nbsp;<a title=\"We love Dealzers deals!\" href=\"http://dealzer.com/?utm_source=HTG&amp;utm_medium=Dealzer&amp;utm_campaign=friends\">Dealzer </a>and <a title=\"SuperCloset - Great guys, great advice.\" href=\"http://supercloset.com/?utm_source=HTG&amp;utm_medium=SuperCloset&amp;utm_campaign=friends\">SuperCloset</a> are second to none – you can have the kit the next day and get growing by the weekend. We have worked all the major supplies over the years and these are the only two companies we recommend, I can honestly say you need to watch your back when dealing with some of the others.</p>\n<p>Or you can save some dollars and piece it together from Amazon or eBay and get a decent system together – it will work and it might be just fine for what you need. Your a word of warning though,&nbsp;we find many of our&nbsp;visitors end up wasting time and money because pieces don’t fit, you buy more than you need, quality is sometimes questionable and advice is zero.</p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element wpb_raw_html\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/Grow-Box-Grow-Tent-2xiygeil1po1v1dsdkj9qi.jpg\" alt=\"HTML Map\" border=\"0\" usemap=\"#html\">\n<!-- Create  Mappings -->\n<map name=\"html\">\n   <area shape=\"rect\" coords=\"1,1,280,390\" href=\"/grow-box\" alt=\"grow-box\" target=\"_self\">\n   <area shape=\"rect\" coords=\"300,1,980,390\" alt=\"grow-tent\" href=\"/grow-tent\" target=\"_self\">\n</map>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"orange button full\"><a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-growing-systems/\" target=\"_self\">Hydroponic Systems – Buyers Reviews</a></div>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><strong>There’s an amazing variety of hydroponic systems available with pros and cons to each. Here we direct you to the reviews.</strong></h2>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Aeroponics system\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/aeroponics\">Aeroponics</a></strong></h2>\n<p>The process of growing marijuana in a fine mist rather than an actual nutrient solution. The roots are confined to a dark, moisture proof area to keep humidity high with intermittent spraying using&nbsp;micro mist nozzles.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Continuous top flow system\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/continuous-flow-hydroponic-system\">Continuous flow / Top feed system</a></strong></h2>\n<p>Using a 2 to 4 inch PVC tube with holes cut in for plants there is a continuous flow of nutrients pumped over the root system. NFT is considered easier.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"DWC system\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/DWC-deep-water-culture\">Deep Water Culture</a></strong></h2>\n<p>(DWC) + Recirculating direct water culture systems (also known as RDWC) + BubblePonics</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Drip irrigation\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/drip-irrigation\">Drip Irrigation</a></strong></h2>\n<p>This is a terrific water/nutrient saving system. Nutrients are dripped right next to the root system which is held in aggregate (medium). There is less evaporation and this system is good for <a title=\"Stealth growing\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/stealth-grow-box\">stealth</a> or apartment growing.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Ebb and flow system\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/ebb-flow-hydroponics-system\">Ebb and Flow</a></strong></h2>\n<p>With pots situated in a tray above a reservoir, the nutrient solution ‘flows’ into the tray and then is allowed to ‘ebb’ away.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Nutrient Film Technique\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/NFT-nutrient-film-technique\">Nutrient Film Technique (NFT)</a></strong></h2>\n<p>Similar to the Ebb and Flow, however the tray above the reservoir is tilted so that a thin film of nutrient flows from the top to drain at the bottom. Nutrient solution is either timed or continuously pumped past the root systems.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Wick hydroponics system\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wick-hydroponic-system\">Wick system</a></strong></h2>\n<p>A very basic system, with either plants all sitting in a medium or within pots situated above the main reservoir and wicks of thick cotton connecting the two. The wick uses capillary action to absorb nutrients up into the medium.</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Sea of Green\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/sea-of-green\">Sea of Green</a></strong> (SoG)</h2>\n<p>A Dutch method to&nbsp;grow marijuana, not so much of a hydroponic system just a method of maximizing crops. The concept is to force the plants to flower when they are very young and small, to push out a sea of green of marijuana plant heads. Got to love the Dutch!</p>\n<h2><strong><a title=\"Screen of Green\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/screen-of-green\">Screen of Green</a></strong>&nbsp;(Screen of Green)</h2>\n<p>Similar to the Sea of Green system except that a screen of chicken wire is placed over the heads of the marijuana to help control and top them.</p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\n\t<div class=\"columns four wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_widgetised_column wpb_content_element\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<ul><li id=\"oio_htg_custom_widget-40\" class=\"widget widget_oio_htg_custom_widget\">\n<ul class=\"oio-banner-zone\" id=\"oio-banner-51\" style=\"width:250px; class=\"wpb_row row brown home-header vc_custom_1403278818986\" style=\"color:#ffffff;\">\n\t<div class=\"columns twelve wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><a href=\"/how-to-grow-marijuana-indoors/\" title=\"\" target=\"_self\" class=\"\"><img wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h1><a name=\"outdoors\"></a><br>\n<a title=\"How to Grow Marijuana Outdoors\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/how-to-grow-marijuana-outdoors/\">Growing Marijuana Outdoors</a></h1>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div><div class=\"wpb_row row\">\n\t<div class=\"columns eight wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\">Growing Marijuana Outdoors</h2>\n<div>\n<h2><strong>Basic requirements</strong>&nbsp;– Marijuana plants need&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-marijuana-ph\">water with the right pH level</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-lighting/\">grow lights</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-nutrients\">nutrients</a>&nbsp;and suitable&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-ventilation-fans-cooling-co2\">air</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hydroponic-ventilation-fans-cooling-co2\">ventilation and temperature</a>. However you choose to <a title=\"Grow marijuana outside\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/how-to-grow-marijuana-outdoors/\">grow&nbsp;marijuana&nbsp;outside</a> you should bear these basic requirements in mind and ask yourself at each stage how can I improve what I offer my plants?</h2>\n<p><strong>Cannabis life cycle outside</strong>&nbsp;– Cannabis is an annual plant and if&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/how-to-grow-marijuana-outdoors/\">grown outside</a>&nbsp;it germinates in the spring, lays down a lot of&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-vegetative-growth-pruning\">vegetative growth</a>&nbsp;throughout the summer, and then&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-flowering\">flowers</a>&nbsp;in the fall. When growing outside it is best to start <a title=\"Germinating marijuana seeds\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/seed-germination\">germinating seeds</a> inside and then planting the seedling at the start of the season in spring. <strong>So germinating your <a title=\"Buy marijuana seeds\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/all-marijuana-strains.html\">marijuana seeds</a> early!</strong></p>\n<p>The season will vary depending on how far you are from the equator and also the elevation of your proposed marijuana garden. Generally you should be able to plant seedlings after&nbsp;the last frost of spring and grow right through to the first hard frost of fall / autumn, specifically the average overnight temperatures should not be below freezing&nbsp;<span style=\"color: #252525;\">32° F or 0° C at any point because that kills marijuana plants.</span></p>\n<p><strong>The main issue growing outdoors is <a title=\"Outdoor marijuana site selection\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/site-selection-preparation\">site selection</a></strong>, security, access to sun throughout the grow (watch out for late in the season and nearby trees) and access to water. If you are <a title=\"Guerilla outdoor growing guide\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/guerilla-grow-guide\">guerilla growing</a> then there will be crucial <a title=\"Outdoor visits\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/visit-growing-weed\">outdoor visits</a>, <a title=\"Marijuana sexing\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-sexing\">sexing marijuana plants</a> and of course the final and delicious <a title=\"Harvesting time\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-harvesting\">harvesting time</a>.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n</div>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> <div class=\"nv-skin mediawrap aligncenter   \"><div class=\"container \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><img src=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wp-content/uploads/outdoor_mj-2xvoqhp4w4ch37hmxdx9my.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"\" height=\"\" style=\"visibility: visible; opacity: 1;\"></div></div></div></div>\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>If you have had a successful vegetative phase then flowering will begin automatically as the days get shorter. Approximately 10 – 12 days after the flowering stage begins you will start to notice two small pistils right at the crux of the branch joint, take a note of the&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-sexing\">sexing marijuana plant pics</a>. To produce the most potent buds it is necessary to remove the male plants as they have very low amounts of THC, CBN and CBD when compared to the females and they will also make the female plants start to seed. Remove the male plants before they pollinate the female plants as once pollinated the females will turn to seed and we don’t want that! The flowers are the bud, the thing we’re looking for and what you will&nbsp;<a href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/harvesting-marijuana-head-body-stone\">harvest</a>&nbsp;and smoke.</p>\n<p>Without males around the female plant will put all of her energy into creating sticky, THC-laden flowers rather than&nbsp;<a title=\"Cannabis seeds\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/all-marijuana-strains/\" target=\"_blank\">cannabis seeds</a>. The result is essentially a virgin plant, or sensimillia, which comes from the Spanish ‘sin semilla’ or ‘without seeds’.</p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element outdoors</a></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> <div class=\"wpb_row row\">\n\t<div class=\"columns twelve tablelayout orange wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\">Marijuana Grow Lights</h2>\n<h2>If you don’t know the difference between <strong><a href=\"/led-grow-lights/\">LED lights</a></strong>, <strong><a href=\"/hid-grow-lights/\">HID lights</a></strong>, <strong><a href=\"/hps-grow-lights/\">HPS lights</a></strong>, <strong><a href=\"/compact-fluorescent-cfl-grow-lights/\">Compact Fluorescent Lights (CFL)</a></strong>&nbsp;or <strong><a href=\"/full-spectrum-led-grow-lights/\">full spectrum lighting</a>&nbsp;or how many plants you can grow under a given light. </strong>What is the difference between, red and blue spectrum, nanometers, Watts, HID/CFL/HPS/MH/LED, light cycles and timings? This knowledge base will help you get to grips with the ins and outs of each, as well as providing ideal sources to get your equipment. <strong>Start here with our <a title=\"Marijuana lighting guide\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/marijuana-lighting/\">Marijuana Lighting Guide.</a></strong></h2>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> <div class=\"nv-skin mediawrap    \"><div class=\"container \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><img src=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wp-content/uploads/mj_lighting-2xvoqgth02m5mv9j8bmoei.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"\" height=\"\" style=\"visibility: visible; opacity: 1;\"></div></div></div></div>\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Whether you need to set up a <a title=\"Stealth grow\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/stealth-grow-box\">small and discrete</a> growing environment or a larger grow space like a <a title=\"Grow tent reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/grow-box\">grow box</a> or huge <a title=\"Grow tent reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/grow-tent\">grow tent</a>, we can recommend the best lighting for your needs and then point you in the right direction where to get them.</p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element wpb_raw_html\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"green button full\"><a title=\"HPS Grow Lights\" href=\"/marijuana-lighting/\">Read more about Grow Lights</a></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  wpb_animate_when_almost_visible wpb_right-to-left\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>LED Grow Lights</h2>\n<p>LED grow lights have been growing marijuana for over a decade now and even <a title=\"NASA uses LED grow lights\" href=\"http://www.nasa.gov/centers/kennedy/home/plant_growth.html\">NASA </a>used them in 2012. LEDs have been in production since 1968 and as the decades progressed LEDs&nbsp;got brighter and cheaper to make.&nbsp;You now see super bright LEDs in car headlamps, stadium lighting and of course LED grow lights.</p>\n<p><strong>The technology is here in a big way and it works, fantastically.</strong> We know one of the best know Dutch seed banks uses them to grow some of their top secret buds, we have seen it with our own eyes and know they work better than HPS. However, not all LEDs are created equal. The cheap ‘purple’ light looking plastic UFO junk are the ones to steer clear of, look for ‘white light’ full spectrum, just like the sun, models with no fans, solid construction, honest specifications and a high end warranty. The full spectrum models in the top end range run nearly cold to touch, save around 50% in electricity and will run for over 12 years growing crops without a single bulb replacement. <strong>We take <a title=\"LED grow light reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/led-grow-lights\">LED grow lights</a> very seriously and <a title=\"LED grow light reviews\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/led-grow-lights\">review all the best models</a> here every year.&nbsp;</strong></p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element wpb_raw_html\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"green button full\"><a title=\"Full Spectrum LED Grow Lights\" href=\"full-spectrum-LED-grow-lights/\">Full Spectrum LED Grow Light Reviews</a></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  wpb_animate_when_almost_visible wpb_left-to-right\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>High Pressure Sodium (HPS) Grow lights</h2>\n<p><a title=\"HPS grow lights\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/hps-grow-lights\">High pressure sodium marijuana grow lights</a> are a good choice for a lot of people, they have been used for growing marijuana indoors for decades. However they are not brilliant at transferring electricity into light and waste a lot of electricity on producing heat instead. <a title=\"LED grow lights\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/led-grow-lights\">LED grow lights</a> are far more efficient at that process. The light HPS&nbsp;emit is also&nbsp;strong&nbsp;in the orange / red spectrum, around 2,200k, due to their inherent sodium content. If a gardener were to start a young plant under a HPS bulb, she/he would see impressive vertical growth so it is why MH lights with their more blue light are often used in the first stages and HPS in the later flowering stages. .</p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  wpb_animate_when_almost_visible wpb_right-to-left\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Metal Halide (MH Grow Lights) – A type of HID</h2>\n<p><strong>MH grow lights</strong> – Metal halide marijuana grow lights primarily emit light in the blue spectrum which promotes excellent photosynthesis and therefore green vegetative growth. Blue light also keeps plants more compact, <strong>it is the closest thing to real sunlight. If you are going to use just one light this is a good compromise.</strong></p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_raw_code wpb_content_element wpb_raw_html\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"green button full\"><a title=\"HPS Grow Lights\" href=\"/marijuana-lighting/\">Free Step by Step Grow Light guide</a></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>LED grow lights vs CFL</h2>\n<p>The compact fluorescent lights (CFL) are a fantastic way to grow in small stealth locations where heat emissions are very important to control, they are cheap to buy and run but they are generally limited on power and that means a poor yield. If you want some more power but still want to maintain a small heat signature, albeit more than CFL you might want to start looking into LEDs – especially the<a title=\"Full spectrum LEDs\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/full-spectrum-LED-grow-lights/\"> full spectrum LEDs</a>. We have a good article here that outlines what you might expect from LEDs there days. <strong><a title=\"LED grow lights\" href=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/led-grow-lights\">More on LED grow lights.</a></strong></p>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div><div class=\"wpb_row row brown home-header vc_custom_1403280221673\">\n\t<div class=\"columns twelve wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"wpb_row row section-header\">\n\t<div class=\"columns three wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"nv-skin mediawrap    \"><div class=\"container \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><a href=\"http://forum.howtogrowmarijuana.com/\" title=\"\" target=\"_self\" class=\"\"><img src=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wp-content/uploads/forum_rev-2xvori4wwyxj48tfpuj1fu.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"\" height=\"\" style=\"visibility: visible; opacity: 1;\"></a></div></div></div></div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\n\t<div class=\"columns nine wpb_column column_container\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h1><a name=\"outdoors\"></a><br>\n<a title=\"The How to Grow Marijuana Forum\" href=\"forum.howtogrowmarijuana.com\" target=\"_blank\">How to Grow Forum</a></h1>\n\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div>\n\t\t</div> \n\t</div> \n</div><div class=\"wpb_row row\">\n\t<div class=\"columns four involved wpb_column column_container vc_custom_1403283378481\">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"nv-skin mediawrap    \"><div class=\"container \"><div class=\"gridimg-wrap\"><div class=\"title-wrap \"><a href=\"http://forum.howtogrowmarijuana.com/\" title=\"\" target=\"_self\" class=\"\"><img src=\"http://howtogrowmarijuana.com/wp-content/uploads/Buddy_forum_Home-2xvok7a0kvvl6r9lxnrbwq.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"\" height=\"\" style=\"visibility: visible;
